 The University of Delhi is going to start a five-year integrated course in journalism from next year by establishing 'delhi School of Journalism' which will provide quality education covering all aspects of journalism
 iske saath hi patrakarita ke maujuuda paathyakram bhi jari rahenge
 In this five-year course to be started under the Delhi School of Journalism, students will have the facility to stop taking a bachelor's degree after three years, or if they wish to complete a post-graduate degree after completing five years
 
 is paathyakram kaa mukhya uddeshy ucch gunvatttapurna shiksha pradaan karne ke liye ek utkrisht kendra sthapit karnaa or yuvaaon ko prashikshan dena he taaki ve kshamta, kaushal or peshevraana ravaiye ke saath is peshey main pravesh kar saken
 Vice Chancellor of Delhi University Yogesh Tyagi said, "the main objective of the proposed 'delhi School of Journalism' in Delhi University is to establish an excellent center for imparting high quality education and training the youth so that they have the ability, skills and professional attitude
 Enter this field with
 ’’ "in this course, some subjects like reporting, editing and photography will remain the same, which are the basic basis of journalism and are taught to the students, but there is also something new that will be completely different," he said
 ’’ Apart from Delhi University, some media houses including Indian Institute of Mass Communication, Jamia Millia Islamia, Indraprastha University, Indira Gandhi Open University, Kendriya Hindi Sansthan and some government and private institutes are running degree and diploma courses in journalism courses
 tippaniyan Savita Dutta, chairman of the committee made on the course outline on the subject of journalism, said, "A five-year curriculum is being prepared which will be completely different from the previous courses at Delhi University
 isamen snaatak or snatakottar donon digriyaan pradaan kii jaaegi
 "it is worth noting that Savita Dutta, the chairman of the committee formed on the subject of journalism, is also the headmistress of the Maitreyi College of Delhi University in Chanakyapuri
 unhone bataaya, ‘‘paathyakram main kya-kya shaamil kiya jaae or kya nahin, iske liye visheshgyon, peshewaron, shikshakon or patrakaron ko baatcheet main shaamil kiya gaya he
 In this course, contemporary and new subjects are also being given place

 Learn 10 special things about Subhash Chandra Bose
 
 
 1
 Subhash Chandra Bose was born on 23 January 1897 in Cuttack, Odisha
 unke pita kaa naam janakinath bose or maa kaa naam prabhavati tha
 Jankinath was a famous lawyer of Cuttack
 2
 After completing primary education in Cuttack, he enrolled in the Revensha Collegiate School
 jiske baad unhone kalakatta uniwarsity se padhai kii
 In 1919, he passed his BA examination from first class, he was ranked second in the university 
 jaane, kaise hui thi rus ko kranti kaa rasta dikhaane vaale lenin kii maut3
 His father wanted Subhash to become ICS
 unhone apane pita kii yah ichha puri kii

 22 april 1921 ko unhone is pad se tyaagptr de diya
 4
 subhash chandra bose kii pehali mulaakaat gandhi ji se 20 july 1921 ko hui thi
 On the advice of Gandhiji, he started working for the Indian freedom struggle
 5
 When he became the principal officer of the Calcutta Municipality, he changed the English name of the routes of Calcutta to the Indian name
 6
 Along with India's independence, their involvement in social work also remained
 bengal kii bhayankar baadh main ghire logon ko unhone bhojan, vastra or surakshit sthanon par pahunchane kaa sahaspurn kaam kiya tha

 7
 They were trying to get Bhagat Singh released from the gallows
 unki rihaai ke liye unhone gandhi ji se baat kii or kaha ki rihaai ke mudde par kiya gaya samjhauta ve angrejon se tod den

 gandhi ji british sarkaar ko diya gaya vachan todane ke liye raji nahin hue, jiske baad bhagat singh ko faansee de di gai
 After this incident he became very angry with the way Gandhi and Congress functioned
 8
 Subhash was sentenced to a total of 11 times in his public life
 sabase pehle unhen 16 july 1921 ko chah maheene kaa karawas diya gaya tha
